ontology layers. graph starts forming meaningful edges.\n\nNow the fun part: the <250ms retrieval.\n\nUser asks something like: “Who am I?”\nThe backend instantly hits a vLLM call to rewrite the query using the user’s persona/context.\n\nThen it runs a hybrid search, grabs all memories that pass the threshold, performs neighborhood traversals on those memories, prolly 3-4 hop (this prevents full graph scanning), It bundles the relevant neighborhood and returns the final context.\n\nFast.  \nClean...\n\nOf course this is a very high level interpretation of what their system might look like, and I’m probably missing pieces.\nMight be naive, might be too semantic based but it makes sense with the latency
